UI/ScreenMatchmaking/AgentsOnLadderOptIn/DetailHeader2=條款與條件 /// Terms & Conditions
UI/ScreenMatchmaking/AgentsOnLadderOptIn/DetailText1=我們很榮幸宣布DeepMind在《星海爭霸II》中的實驗版本人工智慧，AlphaStar，即將以科學研究為目的在天梯上少量進行遊戲。</n></n>如果你想參與DeepMind的研究，和AlphaStar對戰，你可以按下下面的<s val="Versus_AgentsOnLadderOptIn_SectionTextHighlight">參與</s>按鈕。如果你選擇參與並對上了AlphaStar，DeepMind會依照下面的條款使用，或是發表你的對戰資料和戰鬥錄影。我們不會公開發表你的使用者名稱。你可以利用1對1排名對戰功能表中的「參與DeepMind」按鈕，隨時改變你的選擇。</n></n>為了科學實驗目的，DeepMind會匿名使用AlphaStar進行一系列盲測對戰，以衡量系統效能。這表示《星海爭霸》社群成員不會知道AlphaStar參與了那些對戰，以確保每場遊戲都在相同的實驗條件之下。與專業玩家討論過之後，AlphaStar設有限制。對上AlphaStar的對戰，無論輸贏都會如常影響你的對戰積分。</n></n>感謝至今以來協助DeepMind研究和不斷支持的各位，我們會持續探索《星海爭霸》的可能性和極限！ /// We’re excited to announce that experimental versions of DeepMind’s StarCraft II agent, AlphaStar, will soon play a small number of games on the competitive ladder as part of ongoing scientific research into artificial intelligence.</n></n>If you would like the chance to help DeepMind with its research by matching against AlphaStar, you can <s val="Versus_AgentsOnLadderOptIn_SectionTextHighlight">opt-in</s> by clicking the button below. If you opt-in and are matched against AlphaStar, DeepMind will use and may publish your match data and game replays in accordance with the terms below. Your username will not be published.  You can alter your opt-in selection at any time by using the “DeepMind opt-in” button on the 1v1 Versus menu.</n></n>For scientific test purposes, DeepMind will be benchmarking the system’s performance by playing AlphaStar anonymously during a series of blind trial matches. This means the StarCraft community will not know which matches AlphaStar is playing, to help ensure all games are played under the same conditions. AlphaStar plays with built-in restrictions defined in consultation with pro players. A win or a loss against AlphaStar will affect your MMR as normal.</n></n>Thank you to everyone who has helped our work with DeepMind so far, and to all those who continue to support us as we push the boundaries of what’s possible in StarCraft!
UI/ScreenMatchmaking/AgentsOnLadderOptIn/DetailText2=若你在對戰中遇上AlphaStar，DeepMind科技（依英格蘭與威爾斯法律所成立之公司）會使用此遊戲、遊戲錄影，以及所產生的遊戲資料來進行機器學習的發展研究，其中包括發表某些遊戲錄影。</n></n>DeepMind會基於合法利益使用遊戲、遊戲錄影，和遊戲資料中的任何個人資料，以進行機器學習的研究及AlphaStar和其他人工智慧的開發。DeepMind會依照隱私權政策來處理任何個人資料，您可以透過下面的連結檢閱隱私權政策。DeepMind將會是資料控制者。</n></n>如果你改變了與AlphaStar對戰的意願，你可以在任何時間，於對戰畫面選擇參與或退出。 /// If you are matched against AlphaStar, DeepMind Technologies Limited (a company organised under the laws of England and Wales) will use the games, game replays and game data created to conduct research on the development of machine learning, which may include publication of some replays.</n></n>DeepMind will process any personal data contained in games, game replays and game data on the basis of its legitimate interest in pursuing research into machine learning and the further development of AlphaStar and other artificial intelligence agents. DeepMind will handle any personal data in accordance with the privacy policy which can be reviewed using the link below. DeepMind will be a data controller.</n></n>If you change your mind about playing against AlphaStar, you can change your preference to opt-in or opt-out at any time via the Versus screen.

UI/UserProfileLadderDivisionFrame/GrandmasterInfo=宗師聯賽是個尊榮無比的階級，有名額限制，並且只有各地區最頂尖的好手可在此對決，磨礪彼此鬥志並激發潛能。<n/><n/>在新賽季中，要先過了第一週才會決定玩家是否具備晉升到此聯賽的資格。當賽季的第一週結束後，所有的候選人必須再多進行一場對戰才能夠晉升。宗師排名每天都會重新計算，對戰積分不足以進入宗師聯賽的玩家將被剔除，然後由對戰積分達標的玩家遞補。\n\n對戰積分有望爭奪宗師階級的玩家將進入爭奪者名單，玩家在此可更清楚查看所有打算在下一次晉升時爭奪宗師階級的玩家進度如何。降級的玩家將暫時進入爭奪者名單，在當日排名重計前贏得足夠的積分即可返回宗師聯賽。<n/><n/>若要維持在宗師聯賽，每三週最少要進行30場對戰。宗師聯賽不會將獎勵點數納入計算。如果宗師級玩家不夠活躍，將會被自動降級，空出來的名額將由另一名活躍的鬥士遞補。<n/><n/>恭喜那些晉升到宗師聯賽的玩家，祝你們好運！ /// The Grandmaster League is an exclusive league with limited open slots where the top StarCraft II players in each region can compete against each other to test their mettle.<n/><n/>Qualification is determined after the first week in a new season. After the first week, candidates must play one more match in order to receive their promotion. Grandmaster rankings are calculated daily, thus players below the MMR cutoff will be demoted from Grandmaster to make room for those who are above the required MMR threshold.<n/><n/>Players positioned for a spot in Grandmaster will be placed into a Contender List, where they can more easily view the players battling for a coveted slot in the next Grandmaster promotion. Demoted players will have a window of time in the Contender List to earn their spot back before the rankings are calculated for that day.<n/><n/>In order to retain a spot in Grandmaster, a minimum of 30 games every 3 weeks must be played. Bonus pool is not accumulated in Grandmaster. If a player is inactive, they will be automatically demoted and a more active combatant will fill the empty slot.<n/><n/>Congratulations to all those qualified in the Grandmaster League and good luck!
